    // Bootstrap the page with FeatureFlags marked as such.
    window.EM = window.EM || {}
    window.revision = '3.45.2-1bae743f';
    var supported;
    // only support chrome and safari and NOT IE with chromeframe.
    var uAgent = navigator.userAgent;
    switch(true) {
      // ChromeFrame/XX.XX - UNSUPPORTED
      case(/chromeframe\//i.test(uAgent)): {
        supported = false;
        break;
      }
      // Chrome/XX.XX - OK
      case(/chrome\//i.test(uAgent)): {
        supported = true;
        break;
      }
      // Safari/XX.XX - OK
      case (/safari\//i.test(uAgent)): {
        supported = true;
        break;
      }
    }

    // override browser support if we are not the top frame, unless...
    // if (window.self != window.top) supported = false;
    // ...we're in openfin, which gets an iframe pass because reasons...
    if (/openfin/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) supported = true
    // see if something spooked us...
    if (!supported) {
      // manually redirect to "unsupported" page (no backbone routing here)
      // make sure we maintain proper depth in the uri path (dev vs prod)
      // engage...
      window.location.href = "/eikonmessenger/unsupported";
    }
  </script>

      What's New
  
  
  
    <button class="mask-icon close dialog-close-button">×</button>
  
  
  
    </header>
  

  <div class="contents modal-dialog-contents"><div class="notes">
  <div class="whatsNewSection">
    <h2 class="dateHeader">In this release:</h2>
    <ul>
      <li>Bug fixes</li>
    </ul>
  </div>

  <div class="whatsNewSection">
    <h2 class="dateHeader">In previous releases:</h2>
    <ul>
        <li>Bug fixes</li>
    </ul>
    <ul>
        <li>Introducing the new Messenger API for developer use. Eikon Messenger APIs allow you to connect your applications or servers to Eikon Messenger, to improve or automate your workflows. You can find more information at <span class="friendly-link" href="https://developers.refinitiv.com/messenger-api">https://developers.refinitiv.com/messenger-api</span></li>
    </ul>
    <ul>
      <li>Selective printing is now supported; you can highlight a message and right-click to print.</li>
      <li>You can now send a group email to the contacts of your folders.  You can find this option by right-clicking on the folder's name in your Contacts list.</li>
      <li>You can now add a managed chatroom or bilateral chat to an existing Blast window; just drag it from the Contacts list and drop it into the conversation window.</li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Settings improvements</h3>

    <ul>
      <li>Messages posted by external users in chat rooms are now highlighted in red (you can change this in Settings)</li>
      <li>More options are available for the default sound notifications (you can find them under the Alerts settings)</li>
      <li>Standalone Messenger users can now configure the position of toast notifications (Note: enhancement available in the latest standalone Messenger app  - you can download it <span class="friendly-link" href="http://www.myrefinitiv.com">here</span>)</li>
      <li>We also added a Send button in the Message composer.</li>
    </ul>
    <ul>
      <li>Copy a message faster just by highlighting it</li>
      <li>Tidy up your contacts list using our new bulk-remove option for contacts and chatrooms (trash icon at the bottom of your Contacts list)</li>
      <li>The black background is no longer displayed when pasting your messages to other applications</li>
    </ul>
    <ul>
      <li>Our new tool, Message Monitor, lets you see all your incoming messages in one place. To use Message Monitor select the Message Monitor icon on Messenger’s navigation bar.</li>
      <li>Note: Message Monitor is only supported on desktop and in the standalone Messenger app. (You can download the latest standalone Messenger app <span class="friendly-link" href="http://www.myrefinitiv.com">here</span>)</li>
    </ul>
    <ul>
      <li>You can now create a bilateral chat faster by dragging a contact into an existing 1-1 conversation.</li>
      <li>We are also introducing the ability to rename a Chatroom or Bilateral Chat in your own view. Just right-click on the room's name and select the Edit icon in the Profile card.</li>
      <li>You can now see mobile presence indicator for contacts who support offline mobile messaging.</li>
    </ul>
    <ul>
      <li>We now show your top 100 active conversations, from your previous session, when you sign into Messenger (increased from 50).</li>
      <li>When joining a chatroom, you will not see any older messages unless you choose to load more conversation history via the blue link.</li>
      <li>Your chatrooms and bilateral chats will remain in your blast windows even when disconnected - the rooms will be greyed out in the recipients' list of the window while in this state.</li>
    </ul>
    <ul>
      <li>You can now create up to 100 custom groups in your Contacts list.</li><li>
      </li><li>Sound notification enhancements; please contact Support if you experience any issues.</li><li>
      </li><li>Other bug fixes and performance improvements.</li>
    </ul>
    <h3 class="featureHeader">Enhanced Alerting for "In-focus Active Conversations"</h3>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Differentiate External Messages Alerts (1-1 Chats)</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>In Settings -&gt; Alerts -&gt; Event -&gt; Message received in IM -&gt;&nbsp;Differentiate External Messages.</li>
      <li>This feature allows users to configure red alerts whenever message received in 1-1 chats from external users.</li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Differentiate External Messages Alerts (Chat room/Bilateral)</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>In Settings -&gt; Alerts -&gt; Event -&gt; Message received in Chat room -&gt; Differentiate External Messages.</li>
      <li>This feature allows users to configure red alerts whenever message received in chat room/Bilateral from an external users.</li>
      <li>Retain red notification alerts for messages in chat rooms and Bilateral chat.</li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Removing messages in managed chat rooms</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>Chat Room Organizers (CROs) can now remove messages in chat rooms they manage from within Eikon Messenger.</li>
      <li><i>Note: Removed messages will no longer be visible to the chat room participants but will remain available to Compliance officers</i></li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Receiving and delivering offline messages</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>You will now receive messages sent to you while you were offline the next time you log in. Messages sent to an offline contact will also be delivered.</li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Visual enhancements to message delivery status</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>A single check icon is shown next to every sent message, to indicate that it has been delivered to our server.</li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Bold format support</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>Add an asterisk (*) before and after specific words or phrases you want to embolden. e.g. *Hello* or *Good morning!*</li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Flashing notification to indicate new messages in popped-out chat windows</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>Popped-out chats will flash when an incoming message is received.</li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Rename contacts</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>To change a contact’s display name, right-click on the contact and click the ‘pen’ (edit) icon next to the name in the profile card. Type in the new name and press Enter to save.</li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Resize the text box in chat windows</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>To resize the text box to suit your preference, hover over the edge of the box until a double-headed arrow appears. Simply drag upwards or downwards to your desired size. The changes will apply to all chats in the main window. Text boxes in popped-out chat windows can be resized independent of each other.</li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Modify blast window recipients before each blast</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>The recipients list can be modified by checking and un-checking contacts on the participants list in the blast window. </li>
    </ul>

    <h3 class="featureHeader">Keyword alert notification</h3>
    <ul>
      <li>When a contact sends a message with one of your pre-defined keywords in a selected conversation, the keyword will not only be highlighted in the posted message but the unread messages badge will turn yellow.</li>
    </ul>
  </div>
</div>

<button class="button ok">
  OK
</button>

</div>
